SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[GenreName], [v].[Id], [v].[GenreId], [v].[VideoDescription], [v].[VideoName], [v].[VideoUrl]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [g].[Id], [g].[GenreName]
    FROM [Genre] AS [g]
    WHERE [g].[Id] = @__genreId_0
) AS [t]

ORDER BY [t].[Id], [v].[Id]
